colnames(matches_premier_home_score_char)=c('Home_Score','Num_Matches')
matches_premier_home_score_char[order(matches_premier_home_score_char$Home_Score),]

matches_premier_away_score_char = as.data.frame(table(matches_premier$match_awayteam_score), stringsAsFactors = FALSE)
colnames(matches_premier_away_score_char)=c('Away_Score','Num_Matches')
matches_premier_away_score_char[order(matches_premier_away_score_char$Away_Score),]

# Filling the Missing Factors
j = 1
for (i in min(matches_premier$match_hometeam_score) : max(matches_premier$match_hometeam_score))
{ 
    if(matches_premier_home_score_table[j,1] == i)
    {   
        j = j+1
    }
    else
    {#matches_premier_home_score_char[j,] = matches_premier_home_score_table[i,]
        matches_premier_home_score_char[j,1] = matches_premier_home_score_char[j,1]
        matches_premier_home_score_char[j,2] = matches_premier_home_score_char[j,2]
        matches_premier_home_score_char[(j-1),1] = i
        matches_premier_home_score_char[(j-1),2] = 0
    }
}

j = 1
for (i in min(matches_premier$match_awayteam_score) : max(matches_premier$match_awayteam_score))
{ 
    if(matches_premier_away_score_table[j,1] == i)
    {   
        j = j+1
    }
    else
    {#matches_premier_away_score_char[j,] = matches_premier_away_score_table[i,]
        matches_premier_away_score_char[j,1] = matches_premier_away_score_char[j,1]
        matches_premier_away_score_char[j,2] = matches_premier_away_score_char[j,2]
        matches_premier_away_score_char[(j-1),1] = i
        matches_premier_away_score_char[(j-1),2] = 0
    }
}

# Calculating Estimations of Poisson Model for the Dataset

# Getting the Average of HomeTeam Score and AwayTeam Score
print(paste('Number of Matches',nrow(matches_premier)))
matches_premier_home_mean = mean(matches_premier$match_hometeam_score)
matches_premier_away_mean = mean(matches_premier$match_awayteam_score)
print(paste('Home Score Mean is', matches_premier_home_mean))
print(paste('Away Score Mean is', matches_premier_away_mean))
# Calculating Poisson Estimates for HomeTeam Score
print(paste('Home score minimum is', min(matches_premier$match_hometeam_score)))
print(paste('Home score maximum is', max(matches_premier$match_hometeam_score)))
home_poisson_array = vector()
for (i in min(matches_premier$match_hometeam_score) : max(matches_premier$match_hometeam_score))
{ 
    home_poisson_array = c(home_poisson_array, nrow(matches_premier) * dpois(i, lambda=matches_premier_home_mean)) 
}
home_poisson_estimate = data.frame(min(matches_premier$match_hometeam_score) : max(matches_premier$match_hometeam_score),home_poisson_array) 
colnames(home_poisson_estimate)=c('Home_Score','Num_Matches')
home_poisson_estimate[order(home_poisson_estimate$Home_Score),]
home_poisson_estimate

# Calculating Poisson Estimates for AwayTeam Score
print(paste('Away score minimum is',min(matches_premier$match_awayteam_score)))
print(paste('Away score maximum is',max(matches_premier$match_awayteam_score)))
away_poisson_array = vector()
for (i in min(matches_premier$match_awayteam_score) : max(matches_premier$match_awayteam_score))
{ 
    away_poisson_array = c(away_poisson_array, nrow(matches_premier) * dpois(i, lambda=matches_premier_away_mean)) 
}
away_poisson_estimate = data.frame(min(matches_premier$match_awayteam_score) : max(matches_premier$match_awayteam_score),away_poisson_array) 
colnames(away_poisson_estimate)=c('Away_Score','Num_Matches')
away_poisson_estimate

In [ ]:
# bwin, BetOnline, BetGun, Betway were selected
bets_matches_premier_bwin=bets_matches_premier[bets_matches_premier$odd_bookmakers =='bwin',]
# Getting odds
bets_matches_premier_bwin=bets_matches_premier_bwin[bets_matches_premier_bwin$variable=='odd_1'  | bets_matches_premier_bwin$variable=='odd_x' | bets_matches_premier_bwin$variable=='odd_2' ,]

# TASK 2.1
# Calculating Probabilities ,  P(home win), P(tie) and P(away win) by P(x) = 1/odd
bets_matches_premier_bwin$implied_probability=1/(as.numeric(as.character(bets_matches_premier_bwin$value)))
bet_probs_bwin = bets_matches_premier_bwin  %>% group_by(match_id, odd_epoch) %>% summarise(sum(implied_probability))
colnames(bet_probs_bwin)[3]='probability_total'
# TASK 2.2
# Calculating Normalized Probabilities
bets_matches_premier_bwin=merge(x=bets_matches_premier_bwin,y=bet_probs_bwin,by=c('match_id','odd_epoch'),all.x=TRUE)
bets_matches_premier_bwin['norm_prob']=bets_matches_premier_bwin['implied_probability'] * (1/bets_matches_premier_bwin['probability_total'])
bets_matches_premier_bwin_simp = bets_matches_premier_bwin[, c('match_id','odd_epoch','variable','norm_prob')]
bets_matches_premier_bwin_simp = bets_matches_premier_bwin_simp[complete.cases(bets_matches_premier_bwin_simp), ]
bets_matches_premier_bwin_odds = dcast(bets_matches_premier_bwin_simp, match_id + odd_epoch ~ variable, value.var = "norm_prob")
In [ ]:

bets_matches_premier_bwin_odds

bets_matches_premier_bwin_diff=bets_matches_premier_bwin_odds[,c('match_id','odd_epoch','odd_x','Home_Lead')]

# TASK 2.4

In [348]:
# BetOnline
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline=bets_matches_premier[bets_matches_premier$odd_bookmakers =='BetOnline',]
# Getting odds
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline=bets_matches_premier_BetOnline[bets_matches_premier_BetOnline$variable=='odd_1'  | bets_matches_premier_BetOnline$variable=='odd_x' | bets_matches_premier_BetOnline$variable=='odd_2' ,]
# Calculating Probabilities ,  P(home win), P(tie) and P(away win) by P(x) = 1/odd
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline$implied_probability=1/(as.numeric(as.character(bets_matches_premier_BetOnline$value)))
bet_probs_BetOnline = bets_matches_premier_BetOnline  %>% group_by(match_id, odd_epoch) %>% summarise(sum(implied_probability))
colnames(bet_probs_BetOnline)[3]='probability_total'
# Calculating Normalized Probabilities
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline=merge(x=bets_matches_premier_BetOnline,y=bet_probs_BetOnline,by=c('match_id','odd_epoch'),all.x=TRUE)
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline['norm_prob']=bets_matches_premier_BetOnline['implied_probability'] * (1/bets_matches_premier_BetOnline['probability_total'])
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_simp = bets_matches_premier_BetOnline[, c('match_id','odd_epoch','variable','norm_prob')]
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_simp = bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_simp[complete.cases(bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_simp), ]
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_odds = dcast(bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_simp, match_id + odd_epoch ~ variable, value.var = "norm_prob")
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_odds[,"Home_Lead"] = bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_odds[,"odd_1"] - bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_odds[,"odd_2"]  
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_odds
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_diff=bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_odds[,c('match_id','odd_epoch','odd_x','Home_Lead')]
plot(bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_diff[,4],bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_diff[,3],xlab = ' P(home win) – P(away win)',ylab='P (tie)', main='Predictions of BetOnline')
# Adding Bins
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_diff["Bin"] = 0
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_diff$Bin <- cut(bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_diff$Home_Lead, breaks = c(-1, -0.8, -0.6, -0.4, -0.2, 0, 0.2, 0.4, 0.6, 0.8, 1), 
labels = seq(1,10))
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_diff
# Adding Bins and Checking if the Match is Actually Drawn
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_large=merge(x=bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_diff,y=bets_matches_premier_BetOnline[,c('match_id','odd_epoch','match_hometeam_score','match_awayteam_score','norm_prob')],by=c('match_id','odd_epoch'),all.x=TRUE)
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_draw=bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_large[,c('match_id','odd_epoch','match_hometeam_score','match_awayteam_score','norm_prob','Home_Lead','Bin')]
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_draw['is_drawn'] = 0
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_draw['is_drawn'] <- ifelse(bets_matches_premier_BetOnline$match_hometeam_score == bets_matches_premier_BetOnline$match_awayteam_score,1,0)
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_draw
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_draw_prob =bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_draw %>% group_by(Bin) %>% summarise(count=n(),sum(is_drawn))
colnames(bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_draw_prob)[3]='draw'
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_draw_prob$draw_probability=bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_draw_prob$draw/bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_draw_prob$count
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_draw_prob
bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_draw_prob=bets_matches_premier_BetOnline_draw_prob[,c(1,4)]

In [349]:
# BetGun
bets_matches_premier_BetGun=bets_matches_premier[bets_matches_premier$odd_bookmakers =='BetGun',]
# Getting odds
bets_matches_premier_BetGun=bets_matches_premier_BetGun[bets_matches_premier_BetGun$variable=='odd_1'  | bets_matches_premier_BetGun$variable=='odd_x' | bets_matches_premier_BetGun$variable=='odd_2' ,]
# Calculating Probabilities ,  P(home win), P(tie) and P(away win) by P(x) = 1/odd
bets_matches_premier_BetGun$implied_probability=1/(as.numeric(as.character(bets_matches_premier_BetGun$value)))
bet_probs_BetGun = bets_matches_premier_BetGun  %>% group_by(match_id, odd_epoch) %>% summarise(sum(implied_probability))
colnames(bet_probs_BetGun)[3]='probability_total'
# Calculating Normalized Probabilities
bets_matches_premier_BetGun=merge(x=bets_matches_premier_BetGun,y=bet_probs_BetGun,by=c('match_id','odd_epoch'),all.x=TRUE)
bets_matches_premier_BetGun['norm_prob']=bets_matches_premier_BetGun['implied_probability'] * (1/bets_matches_premier_BetGun['probability_total'])
bets_matches_premier_BetGun_simp = bets_matches_premier_BetGun[, c('match_id','odd_epoch','variable','norm_prob')]
bets_matches_premier_BetGun_simp = bets_matches_premier_BetGun_simp[complete.cases(bets_matches_premier_BetGun_simp), ]
bets_matches_premier_BetGun_odds = dcast(bets_matches_premier_BetGun_simp, match_id + odd_epoch ~ variable, value.var = "norm_prob")
bets_matches_premier_BetGun_odds[,"Home_Lead"] = bets_matches_premier_BetGun_odds[,"odd_1"] - bets_matches_premier_BetGun_odds[,"odd_2"]  
bets_matches_premier_BetGun_odds
bets_matches_premier_BetGun_diff=bets_matches_premier_BetGun_odds[,c('match_id','odd_epoch','odd_x','Home_Lead')]
plot(bets_matches_premier_BetGun_diff[,4],bets_matches_premier_BetGun_diff[,3],xlab = ' P(home win) – P(away win)',ylab='P (tie)', main='Predictions of BetGun')
# Adding Bins
bets_matches_premier_BetGun_diff["Bin"] = 0
bets_matches_premier_BetGun_diff$Bin <- cut(bets_matches_premier_BetGun_diff$Home_Lead, breaks = c(-1, -0.8, -0.6, -0.4, -0.2, 0, 0.2, 0.4, 0.6, 0.8, 1), 
labels = seq(1,10))
bets_matches_premier_BetGun_diff
# Adding Bins and Checking if the Match is Actually Drawn
bets_matches_premier_BetGun_large=merge(x=bets_matches_premier_BetGun_diff,y=bets_matches_premier_BetGun[,c('match_id','odd_epoch','match_hometeam_score','match_awayteam_score','norm_prob')],by=c('match_id','odd_epoch'),all.x=TRUE)
bets_matches_premier_BetGun_draw=bets_matches_premier_BetGun_large[,c('match_id','odd_epoch','match_hometeam_score','match_awayteam_score','norm_prob','Home_Lead','Bin')]
bets_matches_premier_BetGun_draw['is_drawn'] = 0
bets_matches_premier_BetGun_draw['is_drawn'] <- ifelse(bets_matches_premier_BetGun$match_hometeam_score == bets_matches_premier_BetGun$match_awayteam_score,1,0)
bets_matches_premier_BetGun_draw
bets_matches_premier_BetGun_draw_prob =bets_matches_premier_BetGun_draw %>% group_by(Bin) %>% summarise(count=n(),sum(is_drawn))
colnames(bets_matches_premier_BetGun_draw_prob)[3]='draw'

In [351]:
# Betway
bets_matches_premier_Betway=bets_matches_premier[bets_matches_premier$odd_bookmakers =='Betway',]
# Getting odds
bets_matches_premier_Betway=bets_matches_premier_Betway[bets_matches_premier_Betway$variable=='odd_1'  | bets_matches_premier_Betway$variable=='odd_x' | bets_matches_premier_Betway$variable=='odd_2' ,]
# Calculating Probabilities ,  P(home win), P(tie) and P(away win) by P(x) = 1/odd
bets_matches_premier_Betway$implied_probability=1/(as.numeric(as.character(bets_matches_premier_Betway$value)))
bet_probs_Betway = bets_matches_premier_Betway  %>% group_by(match_id, odd_epoch) %>% summarise(sum(implied_probability))
colnames(bet_probs_Betway)[3]='probability_total'
# Calculating Normalized Probabilities
bets_matches_premier_Betway=merge(x=bets_matches_premier_Betway,y=bet_probs_Betway,by=c('match_id','odd_epoch'),all.x=TRUE)
bets_matches_premier_Betway['norm_prob']=bets_matches_premier_Betway['implied_probability'] * (1/bets_matches_premier_Betway['probability_total'])
bets_matches_premier_Betway_simp = bets_matches_premier_Betway[, c('match_id','odd_epoch','variable','norm_prob')]
bets_matches_premier_Betway_simp = bets_matches_premier_Betway_simp[complete.cases(bets_matches_premier_Betway_simp), ]
bets_matches_premier_Betway_odds = dcast(bets_matches_premier_Betway_simp, match_id + odd_epoch ~ variable, value.var = "norm_prob")
bets_matches_premier_Betway_odds[,"Home_Lead"] = bets_matches_premier_Betway_odds[,"odd_1"] - bets_matches_premier_Betway_odds[,"odd_2"]  
bets_matches_premier_Betway_odds
bets_matches_premier_Betway_diff=bets_matches_premier_Betway_odds[,c('match_id','odd_epoch','odd_x','Home_Lead')]
plot(bets_matches_premier_Betway_diff[,4],bets_matches_premier_Betway_diff[,3],xlab = ' P(home win) – P(away win)',ylab='P (tie)', main='Predictions of Betway')
# Adding Bins
bets_matches_premier_Betway_diff["Bin"] = 0
bets_matches_premier_Betway_diff$Bin <- cut(bets_matches_premier_Betway_diff$Home_Lead, breaks = c(-1, -0.8, -0.6, -0.4, -0.2, 0, 0.2, 0.4, 0.6, 0.8, 1), 
labels = seq(1,10))
bets_matches_premier_Betway_diff
# Adding Bins and Checking if the Match is Actually Drawn
bets_matches_premier_Betway_large=merge(x=bets_matches_premier_Betway_diff,y=bets_matches_premier_Betway[,c('match_id','odd_epoch','match_hometeam_score','match_awayteam_score','norm_prob')],by=c('match_id','odd_epoch'),all.x=TRUE)
bets_matches_premier_Betway_draw=bets_matches_premier_Betway_large[,c('match_id','odd_epoch','match_hometeam_score','match_awayteam_score','norm_prob','Home_Lead','Bin')]
bets_matches_premier_Betway_draw['is_drawn'] = 0
bets_matches_premier_Betway_draw['is_drawn'] <- ifelse(bets_matches_premier_Betway$match_hometeam_score == bets_matches_premier_Betway$match_awayteam_score,1,0)
bets_matches_premier_Betway_draw
bets_matches_premier_Betway_draw_prob =bets_matches_premier_Betway_draw %>% group_by(Bin) %>% summarise(count=n(),sum(is_drawn))
colnames(bets_matches_premier_Betway_draw_prob)[3]='draw'
bets_matches_premier_Betway_draw_prob$draw_probability=bets_matches_premier_Betway_draw_prob$draw/bets_matches_premier_Betway_draw_prob$count
bets_matches_premier_Betway_draw_prob
bets_matches_premier_Betway_draw_prob=bets_matches_premier_Betway_draw_prob[,c(1,4)]
